### [233] [Scale Buys Interpolation, Structure Buys a Horizon: Certified Predictability for Equivariant World Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13092)
*Hongbo Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种利用等变（Equivariance）结构为世界模型提供可计算、免校准的预测时域证书的方法，证明了结构对于实现可靠预测的重要性，并能够实时审计预训练模型的预测可信度，克服了单纯依靠模型规模难以实现长程可靠预测的局限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大模型在世界建模中存在“规模换取插值”的局限，即平均误差无法反映特定预测在时域上的可信度。现有的世界模型缺乏针对预测时域（Predictable Horizon）的鲁棒性证明和实时审计机制，导致其在实际部署中存在不可控的预测失败风险。

Method: 研究提出了基于等变潜在世界模型的“多步可预测视野证书”。利用李雅普诺夫谱（Lyapunov spectrum）对预测误差进行分层量化，并证明了等变性约束下预测误差在对称轨道上是不变的。通过这一数学特性，在无需训练或校准数据的情况下，对包括TD-MPC2和V-JEPA在内的大规模预训练模型进行实时审计和可靠性评估。

Result: 实验表明，在 Lorenz-96 系统中，仅等变网络能准确恢复李雅普诺夫谱，且在多种预训练模型（TD-MPC2, V-JEPA）上，该方法能有效地自动区分模型的可靠预测区域与过度自信的失效区域，证明了模型性能与参数规模之间并不存在必然的校准关系。

Conclusion: 该研究证实了“规模换取插值，结构换取可信视野”的观点。证明了等变性结构对于获得可靠的预测时域是本质的，非等变模型即使通过增加规模也无法获得这种确定性。该方法无需额外的校准数据，即可为现有世界模型提供实时的、可计算的可信度监控。

Abstract: Scale buys interpolation; structure buys a certified horizon. A world model's average error says nothing about whether a particular prediction can be trusted, or for how long. For equivariant latent world models we give a computable, multi-step certificate of the predictable horizon: $T$-step rollout error is provably constant over each symmetry orbit (Theorem A) and stratified channel-by-channel by the predictor's Lyapunov spectrum, $T_j(ε)\sim\log(1/ε)/λ_j$. The horizon is two-sided -- a matching lower bound makes approximate equivariance provably horizon-limited -- and the certificate is exclusive to structure: orbit-constant error characterizes equivariance, so no non-equivariant model has it at any scale. Empirically, on 40-D Lorenz-96 only a $\mathbb{Z}_N$-equivariant network recovers the full Lyapunov spectrum ($R^2{=}0.98$); dense and recurrent baselines fail.
  Because the spectrum is faithful, the certificate acts, a priori: under a fixed sensing budget a $c\times$-inflated certificate provably needs $c\times$ the budget, and the equivariant certificate meets a budget its inflated dense counterpart cannot -- with zero calibration data. The same read-out, unchanged, audits public pretrained world models training-free: TD-MPC2 checkpoints land on the certificate's own scope taxonomy -- calibrated where strongly expansive (ratio 0.94-1.02), optimistic where weakly expansive, correctly abstaining where contracting -- a map a deployed monitor replicates cell-by-cell, out-of-sample. Across the official 1M-317M multitask ladder, calibration does not improve with parameters. On V-JEPA 2-AC (1B, real robot data) the measured cross-check correctly overrides an over-promising tangent spectrum -- the cross-validated audit, not the raw number, is the deployable object. Scale buys interpolation, not a calibrated horizon.

</details>


### [234] [Authority, Truth, and Citation Bias: A Large-Scale Multi-Domain Benchmark for Studying Epistemic Susceptibility in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13104)
*Aryan Khurana,Aravind Ramana RN,Dhruv Kumar*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 研究揭示了大语言模型存在“权威偏见”，即仅仅通过添加引用（即使是虚假的）就会显著诱发模型产生幻觉，降低其回答的可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前大语言模型在检索增强生成（RAG）场景中应用广泛，但学术界尚未充分理解“引用”这一权威信号本身如何独立于事实内容影响模型的认知行为，即模型是否会因存在引用而更倾向于输出错误信息。

Method: 构建了包含220,564个提示词的AuthorityBench基准测试。采用2x2析因设计，交叉考量“声明真实性”与“引用真实性”。涵盖通用知识、科学、法律和医学四个领域，控制变量包括40种提示模板、四种期刊声望等级及作者人口统计信息。评估了7种主流大模型在12个结构化研究问题上的表现。

Result: 实验发现，无论引用真实与否，只要存在引用，模型的幻觉率均较无引用基线显著上升。其中，在真实声明中附加虚假引用时，幻觉率上升幅度最大（提升3至22个百分点，在通用领域甚至高达35-77%）。此外，法律领域表现相对稳健，而期刊声望和作者人口统计数据对模型行为的影响微乎其微。

Conclusion: 引入引用会诱导大语言模型产生更严重的幻觉，且这种“权威偏见”在引用虚假时尤为明显。这表明模型对引用信号表现出过度的信任，而非基于内容本身的严谨验证。未来的模型训练和评估需重点关注如何减少对外部引用信号的盲目依赖。

Abstract: Large language models are increasingly deployed in citation-augmented settings, yet the effect of citation presence on model behavior independent of factual content remains poorly understood. We introduce AuthorityBench, a 220,564-prompt multi-domain benchmark that isolates how citation-based authority signals influence epistemic behavior in LLMs. The benchmark uses a fully balanced 2x2 factorial design crossing claim veracity with citation veracity, the first to do so, across four domains (general knowledge, science, law, and medicine), with controlled variation over 40 prompt templates, four venue prestige tiers, and a country-coded author name dataset. Evaluating seven models on 12 structured research questions, we find that citation presence, whether real or fabricated, consistently increases hallucination rates relative to a no-citation baseline. The effect is strongest when fabricated citations accompany true claims, raising hallucination rates by 3 to 22 percentage points and reaching 35 to 77% in the general knowledge domain, while legal claims are comparatively robust and venue prestige and author demographics show negligible impact. All datasets and evaluation code are available at: https://github.com/floating-reeds/AuthorityBench

### [235] [Disparate Impact in Synthetic Data Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13105)
*Paul Andrey,Michaël Perrot,Batiste Le Bars,Marc Tommasi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究重新定义了合成数据生成（SDG）中的公平性问题，认为公平应建立在精准拟合真实数据分布的基础上。通过分析模型误差来源，作者提出了一种分组建模策略，有效缓解了合成数据在不同群体间的效用差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究多通过修正原始数据分布来实现合成数据的公平性，但这本质上是生成与原始分布不同的数据。本文旨在重新审视这一公平性概念，指出当合成数据分布与真实数据分布一致时，差异影响才会消失，并探究导致模型在不同群体间表现不一致的深层技术原因。

Method: 本文通过分析概率图模型，探讨了合成数据生成（SDG）中模型表现力不足、样本规模差异导致的采样误差以及差分隐私机制引入的估计误差。在此基础上，提出了一种基于分组（group-wise）的SDG学习策略，旨在减少各组间效用的不均衡。

Result: 研究发现，SDG模型在不同群体间的表现差异主要受限于模型的表达能力、群体样本比例导致的采样噪声以及差分隐私带来的估计误差。实验结果表明，采用分组建模的SDG方法能显著改善各群体间的效用公平性及其整体性能。

Conclusion: 本文指出，合成数据生成中的差异影响（Disparate Impact）本质上源于估计与近似误差，而非训练数据本身的不当偏差。通过采用分组建模策略，可以在保持模型对真实数据分布忠诚度的同时，有效提升公平性与整体效用。

Abstract: We revisit the fairness notion of disparate impact for synthetic data generation (SDG), that assesses whether the utility of generated records is the same across sensitive groups. Our approach departs from existing work on fair SDG, that address the problem of correcting for undue biases in the observed distribution, hence redefining SDG as learning a distribution that is not that of the real data. By contrast, non-disparate impact is notably achieved when the synthetic and real distributions are the same. We expose reasons why SDG may fail to reach that solution and discuss why approximation and estimation errors occur and can be disparate across groups. We notably look into the expressive power of SDG methods relative to distribution complexity, sampling errors due to group proportions, and estimation errors induced by differential privacy mechanisms. We illustrate cases of disparate impact on both artificial and real-world data, focusing on SDG methods that rely on probabilistic graphical models. We also introduce a strategy of learning group-wise SDG models and illustrate how it can improve both the overall utility and its parity in many settings.

### [236] [Demystifying Hidden-State Recurrence: Switchable Latent Reasoning with On-Policy Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13106)
*Jiayu Yang,Chao Chen,Shengen Wu,Yinhong Liu,Yuxuan Fan,Lujundong Li,Songning Lai,Chengwei Qin,Zhijiang Guo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SWITCH通过在潜在推理过程中引入显式边界标记（<swi>...</swi>），解决了传统潜在推理方法难以进行强化学习训练且无法解释的问题，实现了高效、可优化且可解释的潜在思维链推理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的潜在思维链（Latent CoT）方法虽能压缩推理过程，但存在两大痛点：一是难以通过标准的同策略强化学习（On-policy RL）进行优化，二是其内部过程缺乏因果可解释性。作者试图通过引入显式边界标记来同时解决这两个问题。

Method: 提出了SWITCH框架：引入<swi>和</swi>作为潜在推理的显式边界标记，使其与标准策略优化（如GRPO）兼容；采用“可见到潜在”的课程学习策略，并使用Switch-GRPO目标函数通过循环潜在计算进行梯度传播；利用边界标记进行直接探测和因果干预分析。

Result: SWITCH在同等规模下持续优于现有的潜在推理方法；机制分析揭示了<swi>不仅是学习到的切换策略，其触发的潜在步骤执行了特定问题的关键计算，且计算集中在进入时刻的单一隐藏状态转换上。

Conclusion: SWITCH框架证明了潜在推理（hidden-state recurrence）可以通过离散边界标记（boundary tokens）实现高效的强化学习训练，并且可以通过机制可解释性分析揭示潜在推理的内部运作机理，打破了“潜在推理不可解释”的传统观念。

Abstract: Latent chain-of-thought compresses reasoning by replacing visible reasoning traces with continuous hidden-state recurrence, but existing formulations are difficult to optimize with standard on-policy reinforcement learning (RL) and hard to interpret causally. Our key insight is that a single pair of explicit boundary tokens can address both issues at once: discrete entry and exit anchors make the latent block compatible with standard on-policy RL, and the same anchors offer a natural foothold for mechanistic analysis. Motivated by this, we propose SWITCH, a switchable latent reasoning framework. The model emits <swi> to enter latent mode and </swi> to exit. Because the boundaries are ordinary discrete tokens, the GRPO policy ratio is well-defined at every decision point. The same anchors also expose the latent steps to direct probing and causal intervention. We train the model with a visible-to-latent curriculum and a Switch-GRPO objective that propagates gradients through recurrent latent computation. SWITCH consistently outperforms prior hidden-state-recurrence latent reasoning approaches at similar scale. Mechanistic analysis through the boundary tokens further reveals three findings: (i) <swi> is a sharply localised, learned switching policy rather than a stylistic artefact; (ii) the latent step it opens performs problem-specific, causally important computation rather than acting as an inert placeholder; and (iii) that computation is concentrated at a single hidden-state transition on entry. Together, these results show that hidden-state-recurrence latent reasoning is both RL-trainable and open to direct mechanistic analysis, including of how on-policy RL itself improves the model from the inside.

### [237] [MP3: Multi-Period Pattern Pre-training forSpatio-Temporal Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13119)
*Lilan Peng,Yandi Liu,Qingren Yao,Chongshou Li,Tianrui Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为MP3的即插即用预训练插件，专门用于解决时空预测中的“时间海市蜃楼”难题，通过建模多周期模式并增强跨周期交互，显著提升了现有各类时空图神经网络的预测精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有STGNN模型难以识别城市时空数据中的“时间海市蜃楼”现象（即相似短窗口输入对应不同未来趋势，或不同输入对应相似趋势）。作者认为其根本原因是短窗口输入导致了周期观测不完整、空间相关性异构以及跨周期因果干扰。

Method: MP3包含两个核心创新点：1. 多周期模式学习：通过边缘卷积对长时序进行多周期建模，利用瓶颈投影和全局记忆库捕捉异构空间关联，并利用因果增强Transformer处理跨周期模式交互；2. 插件式架构：设计为一种即插即用的预训练模块，可无缝集成到现有多种时空图神经网络（STGNN）骨干模型中，增强其对复杂时空规律的辨识能力。

Result: 在五个真实世界数据集上，对五个STGNN基准模型进行了测试。实验结果表明，MP3能稳定提升所有基准模型的性能，平均MAE降低了4.7%，RMSE降低了5.0%，验证了该方法的高效性、可扩展性和适应性。

Conclusion: MP3通过引入多周期模式预训练插件，有效解决了现有STGNN在处理时空数据“时间海市蜃楼”现象时的局限性。该方法具备即插即用的特性，不仅能显著提升多种主流时空预测模型的性能，还展现了良好的泛化能力和可扩展性。

Abstract: Spatio-Temporal forecasting is crucial in diverse fields, such as transportation, climate, and energy. Urban spatio-temporal data exhibits temporal mirage: similar short-window inputs have divergent future trends, and vice versa. Existing spatio-temporal graph neural networks (STGNNs) cannot effectively identify such mirages. We argue that the core reason lies in the short-window inputs that have incomplete period observation, heterogeneous global spatial correlation, and cross-period superposition causality. To bridge this gap, we develop a novel Multi- Period Pattern Pre-training (MP3), a plug-and-play pre-training plugin for distinguishing temporal mirages. MP3 presents two core innovations: (1) The multi-period pattern learning is designed to learn multi-period patterns from long time series. Specifically, multi-period temporal modeling leverages edge convolution to identify different multi-period patterns. Multi-period spatial modeling uses a bottleneck project and a global memory bank to capture heterogeneous global spatial relations efficiently. Cross-period pattern interaction employs a causality-enhanced Transformer to capture dependencies across different period patterns. (2) This plugin can seamlessly integrate into existing STGNN backbones to strengthen their forecasting performance. The experiment on five STGNN baselines across five real-world datasets (including a large-scale dataset CA) verify the effectiveness, superior scalability and strong adaptability of MP3, which brings consistent and robust performance improvements across all evaluated baselines. On average, MP3 reduces the MAE 4.7% and the RMSE 5.0%. The code can be available at https://github.com/YAN-outlook/MP3.

### [238] [Select and Improve: Understanding the Mechanics of Post-Training for Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13125)
*Akshay Krishnamurthy,Audrey Huang,Nived Rajaraman*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过对 Qwen-2.5-1.5B 进行受控实验，揭示了强化学习后训练提升推理能力的两个核心机制：通过多样化SFT数据实现“策略选择”，以及通过难度递增的强化学习数据实现“策略改进”。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 研究识别出两个核心机制：1. 策略选择（Strategy Selection）：通过监督训练（SFT）阶段提供多样的推理策略，使模型能够学会在面对问题时进行有效选择；2. 策略改进（Strategy Improvement）：通过在强化学习阶段利用由浅入深的难度递增数据，促使模型优化现有的推理逻辑。

Conclusion: 强化学习后训练在提升模型推理能力中扮演了关键角色，其本质在于通过策略选择与策略改进两个核心机制的协同作用。研究表明，通过优化SFT阶段的数据多样性与RL阶段的任务难度，可以有效驱动这些机制，从而为推理能力的持续规模化提供了明确的路径。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning has rapidly emerged as a key component in the training of reasoning and coding models, yet it remains poorly understood from a mechanistic perspective. We study how and through what underlying processes capabilities are acquired or enhanced via reinforcement learning post-training. Our analysis, based on controlled math reasoning experiments with Qwen-2.5-1.5B, reveals two core mechanisms: strategy selection and strategy improvement. Our results highlight the role of SFT data and reinforcement learning data in activating these mechanisms, in particular showing how supervising the model on diverse reasoning strategies can enable strategy selection and how increasing difficulty in reinforcement learning data can enable strategy improvement. Taken together, our results provide mechanistic insight into RL training and suggest practical interventions to continue scaling reasoning capabilities.

### [239] [MiniPIC: Flexible Position-Independent Caching in <100LOC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13126)
*Nathan Ordonez,Thomas Parnell*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: MiniPIC 是一种轻量级的 vLLM 扩展，通过解耦位置编码和引入用户可控的缓存原语，实现了高效的位置无关 KV 缓存重用，在大幅提升 RAG 类工作负载的推理效率的同时，保持了极低的实现复杂度和运行开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在检索增强生成（RAG）和智能体任务中，系统经常处理重复的结构化输入（如文档、代码）。现有的 vLLM 引擎通过前缀缓存（Prefix Caching）虽然可以重用 KV，但要求请求拥有完全相同的前缀，而现有的位置无关缓存（PIC）方案往往需要大规模改动服务器代码，或者存在高昂的设备间数据传输开销。MiniPIC 旨在解决这些限制，在不大幅改变系统架构的前提下实现高效的 KV 缓存重用。

Method: MiniPIC 的核心方法包括：1. 位置编码无关的 KV 缓存（存储未旋转的 K 向量，在注意力计算内部按需应用 RoPE）；2. 三种用户可控的底层原语：块对齐填充（Block-aligned padding）、跨度分隔符（SSep）和提示依赖（PDep）。这些机制允许用户精细控制缓存的哈希行为和因果注意力结构，从而支持多种位置无关缓存（PIC）策略。

Result: 在 2WikiMultihopQA 数据集上的测试表明，MiniPIC 在交叉调度下将预填充吞吐量提升了 49%，将已缓存跨度的首字延迟（TTFT）降低了多达两个数量级，且最坏情况下的系统开销仅为 5.7%。此外，它在保持线性预填充缩放性能的同时，完美支持了现有的 CPU 卸载实现。

Conclusion: MiniPIC 提供了一种轻量级、灵活且高效的缓存机制，能够无缝集成到 vLLM 中。通过仅修改少量代码，它实现了位置无关的缓存，不仅大幅提升了长文本和检索增强型任务的预填充吞吐量，还显著降低了首字延迟，为生产环境中的高效大模型推理提供了强有力的支持。

Abstract: Retrieval-augmented and agentic workloads repeatedly prefill recurring predictable structured inputs (which we call "spans") such as documents and code files. Yet, prefix caching in engines such as vLLM cannot reuse their KV entries unless they share identical prefixes with another request, while Position-Independent Caching (PIC) implementations within production-grade inference servers typically either require substantial server code changes or keep KV state outside the server, incurring host-to-device transfer overhead. We present Minimalistic PIC (MiniPIC): a minimal, flexible and fast vLLM design built from two ingredients: positional-encoding-free KV cache and user-controlled cache-reuse primitives. MiniPIC stores unrotated K vectors in the KV cache, applies RoPE to K tiles inside attention using per-request logical positions, and exposes three user-facing and token-level primitives: block-aligned padding, span separator (SSep), and prompt depend (PDep), that modify hashing behavior and effective block-level causal attention structure. With fewer than 100 lines of core-engine changes plus a custom attention backend, these primitives are sufficient to realize multiple PIC methods, including Block-Attention, EPIC, and Prompt Cache, within the same running vLLM instance, while natively integrating with KV cache CPU offload implementations. On 2WikiMultihopQA, MiniPIC with interleaved scheduling improves prefill throughput by 49% over baseline vLLM, reduces cached-span time-to-first-token by up to two orders of magnitude, preserves the linear prefill scaling of uncached spans, and incurs only 5.7% worst-case overhead.

</details>


### [240] [When Does Routing Become Interpretable? Causal Probes on Block Attention Residuals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13168)
*Aydin Javadov*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了“块注意力残差”（Block AttnRes）机制是否能提升模型的可解释性。结论指出，虽然该架构使跨层路由变得可视化，但路由权重大小并不直接等同于路径的因果重要性；因此，仅凭可视化路由不足以解释模型机制，必须通过因果干预进行验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的神经网络残差连接机制（如ResNet）通常是固定且不可见的，而“块注意力残差”（Block AttnRes）通过学习softmax加权整合早期层表示，使跨层路由成为前向传播中可观测的张量。研究动机在于探讨这种架构上的显式路由暴露，是否足以实现对模型机制的直观解释。

Method: 研究者对比了两个规模相同（0.6B参数）的Qwen3模型：一个是使用确定性“近因偏差”调度封装的普通模型（作为基准），另一个是从零开始训练、将路由作为优化目标的Block AttnRes模型。研究通过路由消融干预（routing-ablation interventions）来对比两者的信息流动，并分析路由权重与因果贡献之间的关系。

Result: 1. 经过训练的Block AttnRes模型表现出三种局部路由模式：早期的嵌入源路径、早期的当前状态路径以及后期的历史信息路径；2. 发现路由权重（即路由质量）与因果重要性之间存在明显解耦；3. 即使路由权重很大，也不代表该路径具有因果贡献，存在大量占用路由权重但对模型输出无实际因果影响的路径。

Conclusion: 架构上的路由信息暴露是进行机制可解释性分析的必要条件，但并非充分条件。仅凭路由权重分布（描述性摘要）不足以推断模型机制，研究人员必须将其视为待验证的假设，并通过因果干预手段进行严格测试。此外，结构化的深度路由行为仅在训练过程中明确优化该机制时才会出现。

Abstract: Block Attention Residuals (Block AttnRes) by replace fixed additive residuals with a learned softmax over earlier depth-source representations, surfacing cross-layer routing as an inspectable tensor in the forward pass. This is a tempting interpretability target: information flow normally inferred indirectly is now directly observable. We ask whether such exposure suffices for mechanistic interpretation. We probe two same-scale ($0.6$B) Block AttnRes checkpoints under identical routing-ablation interventions: a vanilla Qwen3 inference-wrapped through a deterministic recency-bias schedule that the codebase admits as a routing-equivalent loading path, and a Block AttnRes Qwen3 trained from scratch with routing as part of optimisation. The wrapped baseline's routing weights are content-independent and reproduce the schedule's analytic prediction. The trained AttnRes checkpoint instead exhibits three localised routing motifs: an embedding-source pathway through early-layer MLP, a current-state pathway through early-layer attention and MLP, and an older-history pathway through late-layer attention. Beyond this stratification, we find a sharp dissociation between average routing mass and causal importance: in both sublayers, the largest mass slice is not the largest causal contribution, and one source family carries appreciable mass with no detectable causal role under intervention. Architectural exposure of routing is therefore necessary but not sufficient for mechanistic interpretation: structured depth routing emerges only when routing has been part of training, and even then, descriptive routing summaries should be treated as candidate hypotheses to be tested by causal interventions, not as evidence of mechanism in their own right.

</details>

*Jacques Raynal,Pierre Slangen,Elsa Raynal,Jacques Margerit*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的评估指标（如预测准确率、鲁棒性等）无法完全捕捉表示学习中潜在的、未能被模型充分解释的残差结构，导致模型虽在指标上表现成功，但在解释深度和结构洞察上存在不足。

Method: 提出 VER（表示警惕评估器）框架，该框架包含一套系统的诊断流程：表示识别、解释域划分、残差结构检测、解释阻力评估以及警惕信号触发，旨在将表示的充分性作为独立的评估对象。

Result: 建立了一套诊断机制，能够有效区分“表示不充分”与普通的预测误差、不确定性或数据分布偏移，并为未来的“表示警惕性基准测试”提供了方法论基础。

Conclusion: VER 为机器学习模型的表示诊断提供了一个补充性的评估框架，强调通过监控残差结构来识别现有模型在解释性上的不足，从而促进构建更鲁棒、更具解释力的表示学习方法。

Abstract: Learned representations are central to modern machine learning and are commonly evaluated through predictive performance, robustness, uncertainty estimation, or generalization. However, a learned representation may remain operationally successful while progressively failing to organize persistent residual structures that are not fully captured by conventional evaluation metrics. This article introduces VER, the Vigilant Evaluator of Representations, a conceptual framework for monitoring representational adequacy in learned representations. VER does not propose a new learning algorithm, loss function, or model architecture. Instead, it formalizes a diagnostic process through which persistent residual structures may be identified, analyzed, and interpreted as potential indicators of explanatory insufficiency. The framework distinguishes representational inadequacy from ordinary prediction error, uncertainty, noise, and distribution shift. It introduces a monitoring sequence based on representation identification, explanatory-domain delimitation, residual-structure detection, explanatory-resistance evaluation, and vigilance signaling. VER is intended as a contribution to representation diagnostics in machine learning. Its objective is not to replace existing evaluation methods but to complement them by treating representational adequacy as an explicit object of inquiry. A path toward empirical evaluation through representational-vigilance benchmarks is also outlined.

### [242] [Getting Better at Working With You: Compiling User Corrections into Runtime Enforcement for Coding Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13174)
*Yujun Zhou,Kehan Guo,Haomin Zhuang,Xiangqi Wang,Yue Huang,Zhenwen Liang,Pin-Yu Chen,Tian Gao,Nuno Moniz,Nitesh V. Chawla,Xiangliang Zhang*

TL;DR: 本文提出了TRACE方法，旨在解决LLM代理无法长期遵循用户偏好纠正的问题。通过将用户纠正转化为强制性的编译规则，TRACE显著提高了代理在多次会话中的偏好合规性，减少了用户重复反馈的负担。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前的交互式LLM代理在处理长期记忆时存在缺陷，用户在一次会话中的纠正往往无法在后续会话中保持，导致用户需要反复重复相同的偏好，即使使用Mem0等内存方案，偏好违规率依然较高。

Method: 提出了TRACE（Test-time Rule Acquisition and Compiled Enforcement）技术管道。该方法通过挖掘用户在交互中的纠正意见，将其重写为原子级规则，并编译为代理运行时的强制检查机制，确保代理在完成后续任务前必须满足这些用户设定的偏好。

Result: 在ClawArena编码任务中，TRACE将同分布任务的违规率从100%降至37.6%，跨分布任务从100%降至2.0%；在MemoryArena任务中，违规率从100%降至60.5%，且在任务完成质量上表现出色。

Conclusion: 将用户的反馈纠正转化为原子规则并进行编译时强制执行（TRACE），能够有效弥补现有LLM代理内存机制的不足，显著降低偏好违规率，实现用户只需“告知一次”即可长期生效，从而提升代理在后续任务中的可靠性。

Abstract: Interactive LLM agents are becoming part of daily work, but they do not reliably become easier to work with over time: a correction remembered in one session may still be violated in the next. We study this gap between preference access and preference compliance. In tasks derived from anonymized real-user friction cases, Mem0 memory still leaves 57.5% of applicable preference checks violated. We introduce Test-time Rule Acquisition and Compiled Enforcement (TRACE), a drop-in skill-layer pipeline for coding-agent runtimes that mines user corrections, rewrites them as atomic rules, and compiles them into runtime checks that must pass before an agent completes future tasks. Unlike runtime checks written ahead of time by developers, TRACE skills come from the user's own chat corrections. We evaluate TRACE with simulated user-in-the-loop experiments on ClawArena coding-agent tasks and MemoryArena-derived memory-intensive tasks. On ClawArena, TRACE reduces held-out preference violation from 100.0% to 37.6% on in-distribution tasks and from 100.0% to 2.0% on out-of-distribution tasks. On MemoryArena-derived tasks, TRACE reduces in-distribution violation from 100.0% to 60.5% while matching or exceeding the strongest memory baseline on task pass. These results suggest that compiling corrections into runtime enforcement can address a repeated-friction failure mode that memory alone does not reliably solve, reducing the need for users to restate the same correction across future sessions. Experiment code is available at https://github.com/YujunZhou/TRACE_exp, and the deployable skill is available at https://github.com/YujunZhou/tellonce.

### [243] [Understanding helpfulness and harmless tension in reward models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13209)
*Eshaan Tanwar,Pepa Atanasova*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究通过机制可解释性手段揭示了RLHF奖励模型中“有用性”与“无害性”目标之间的内部冲突，发现共享神经元的相互干扰是导致对齐张力的主要原因。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: RLHF中奖励模型（Reward Models）如何平衡“有用性”与“无害性”的内部机制尚不明确，且混合目标训练中常出现性能干扰。研究旨在揭示这种对齐张力的机理，并从可解释人工智能的角度解析多目标对齐的困难所在。

Method: 1. 对比分析法：训练有用性导向、无害性导向以及混合目标的奖励模型，比较其性能差异。
2. 激活分析法：利用激活分析定位与特定目标相关的关键神经元。

Result: 1. 混合目标模型在单一指标上的表现通常逊色于单一目标模型，证实了目标间的干扰。
2. 识别出负责特定目标的神经元，这些神经元在支持自身目标的同时，往往会对另一个目标产生负面影响。
3. 存在大量共享神经元，这些神经元对模型行为影响巨大，且是导致对齐目标冲突的关键因素。

Conclusion: 研究表明，奖励模型中“有用性”与“无害性”目标之间存在显著的对齐张力（Alignment Tension）。这种张力源于神经元层面的功能冲突与重叠，尤其是共享神经元的负面干扰机制。该发现为开发更具可解释性、解耦且可控的对齐技术奠定了理论基础。

Abstract: Reward models are a key component of reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF), aligning language models toward both helpful and harmless behaviour. However, the internal mechanisms underlying these objectives and their conflicts remain poorly understood. We study alignment tension in reward models trained under helpfulness-only, harmlessness-only, and mixed-objective settings. We find that mixed-objective models often underperform single-objective models, indicating interference between objectives. Using activation-based methods, we identify neurons associated with each objective and study their functional roles via targeted ablations. We find that these neurons causally support their corresponding objectives while often negatively affecting the opposing one. We find that a substantial proportion of neurons are shared between helpfulness and harmlessness, and that these shared neurons exert a disproportionate influence on model behaviour, contributing to alignment tension. Additionally, our results provide insights and mechanistic interpretation into how alignment objectives are represented in reward models and why multi-objective alignment remains challenging, motivating future work on disentangled and controllable alignment methods.

### [244] [Loss-Shift Transfer via Bayes Quotients](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13178)
*Vasileios Sevetlidis*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文探讨了“损失偏移”现象，指出即使数据分布一致，损失函数的差异也会导致迁移学习失效；作者通过贝叶斯商理论分析了损失函数的精细度，并证明了表征所丢失的信息直接决定了其在不同损失函数下的性能表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的迁移学习研究多关注数据分布偏移（distribution shift），但作者指出存在另一种正交的失败模式：即在数据分布固定时，由于目标任务使用的损失函数（loss）不同，导致原有的表征失效。研究旨在形式化描述这种“损失偏移”现象及其对模型性能的影响。

Method: 1. 定义了“损失偏移”（loss shift）概念，将其作为分布偏移之外的独立失败模式。
2. 引入“贝叶斯商”（Bayes quotients）数学框架，将损失函数按精细程度进行排序。
3. 推导出针对有限输出对数损失的定量恒等式，将超额风险（excess risk）与表征丢弃的条件信息量挂钩。
4. 在受控合成数据及真实图像设置中进行了实验验证。

Result: 1. 理论上证明了当目标损失比源损失更“精细”时，源任务训练出的最优表征无法满足目标任务的要求。
2. 对于有限输出的对数损失，量化了表征丢失信息与超额风险之间的关系。
3. 实验证实了分类等价的表征在面对不同的对数损失时，其最优性能存在显著差异。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了即使在数据分布不变的情况下，损失函数的变化也会导致表征学习的失败。通过贝叶斯商（Bayes quotients）这一理论工具，研究证明了损失函数的精细程度直接决定了所需表征的充分性。这一发现对于理解迁移学习中“损失偏移”带来的表征失效具有深远的理论指导意义。

Abstract: Transfer learning is usually studied as a consequence of distribution shift. This paper identifies an orthogonal failure mode in which the data distribution is fixed and the loss changes. This setting is called \emph{loss shift}. A loss determines which information in \(X\) is Bayes-relevant, and two losses may therefore require different representations even under the same joint law \(P(X,Y)\). The idea is formalized using Bayes quotients, which allow losses to be ordered by refinement. In the Bayes-quotient formulation, strict refinement gives an immediate qualitative obstruction. A source-minimal representation for a coarser loss is insufficient for a strictly finer target loss. For finite-output log loss, this obstruction becomes an exact quantitative identity. The excess risk is the conditional information about \(Y\) discarded by the representation. Experiments in controlled, learned, synthetic-image, and real-image settings show the predicted effect, i.e., classification-equivalent representations can have different optimal log-loss performance under a fixed data distribution.

</details>


### [245] [The Geometry of Phase Transitions in Generative Dynamics via Projection Caustics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13191)
*Ryosuke Sakamoto,Kotaro Sakamoto*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文揭示了扩散模型生成过程中的“突然变化”源于几何焦散现象，并据此提出了一种名为CBD的诊断工具，用于定位和控制扩散模型中的模态选择与生成不稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管扩散模型和流匹配模型基于连续时间的演化动力学，但其生成过程中往往出现突然的质量变化或模态坍缩。作者希望从几何角度解释这种类似“相变”的行为，从而量化并控制生成过程中的敏感时间窗口。

Method: 1. 理论建模：将去噪过程解释为在自由能景观上的梯度下降；2. 几何分析：引入微分几何中的“焦散（caustics）”概念，分析最近点投影在数据支持集上的非唯一性，解释为何模型在特定时间窗内会发生剧烈的质变；3. 工具开发：提出“临界边界检测器（CBD）”，用于检测分数方向（score-direction）的不稳定性，定位模型对干预敏感的区域。

Result: 研究表明，生成过程中的不稳定性与数据流形的投影焦散点高度相关。CBD工具在玩具模型、标准扩散模型及潜在空间文生图模型中表现优异，能够精确定位模态确认的时间点，预测干预敏感区，并支持在几何敏感区域进行定向控制。

Conclusion: 本研究成功将扩散模型的生成过程与微分几何中的焦散理论联系起来，证明了扩散模型中的“模态承诺”现象本质上是由于数据流形上的几何奇点（焦散点）所致。CBD诊断工具为理解和调控生成过程提供了有效的几何视角，有助于提升扩散模型的生成可控性。

Abstract: Continuous-state generative samplers, including diffusion and flow-matching models, evolve through continuous reverse-time dynamics, yet their samples often undergo abrupt qualitative changes: trajectories commit to modes, semantic alternatives collapse, and small perturbations in narrow time windows can produce large downstream effects. This paper develops a geometric account of such phase-transition-like behaviour. We view denoising as gradient descent on a free energy landscape and show that sharp transitions arise near projection caustics, where the nearest-point projection onto the data support ceases to be unique. Motivated by this perspective, we introduce the Critical Boundary Detector (CBD), as practical diagnostics for score-direction instability. Across toy models, standard diffusion models, and latent text-to-image diffusion models, CBD localises mode commitment, predicts intervention-sensitive windows, and supports targeted control in geometrically sensitive regions. Our results connect geometry of data and dynamics of diffusion generation.

### [246] [MaxProof: Scaling Mathematical Proof with Generative-Verifier RL and Population-Level Test-Time Scaling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13473)
*Jiacheng Chen,Xinyu Zhang,Shunkai Zhang,Yanmohan Wang,Lin Li,Tiancheng Qin,Qin Wang,Zhengmao Zhu,Tianle Li,Jingyang Li,Zehan Li,Binyang Jiang,Jin Zhu,Han Ding,Fei Yu,Chenyu Du,Zijian Song,Jiayuan Song,Zhi Zhang,Yunan Huang,Weiyu Cheng,Pengyu Zhao,Yu Cheng*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文介绍了 MaxProof，这是一个用于竞赛级数学证明的测试时扩展框架，通过生成、验证、修复及种群搜索策略，使 M3 模型在 IMO 和 USAMO 等高难度数学竞赛中达到并超过了人类金牌水平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了解决语言模型在处理竞赛级复杂数学证明时准确性不足的问题，通过开发一套能够在推理阶段进行自我迭代、验证和优化的系统，以提升模型的数学逻辑推理上限。

Method: 提出 MaxProof 框架，包含三个核心能力：证明生成、证明验证和基于批判（critique）的修复；利用深度防御（defense-in-depth）的生成式验证器降低误报率；在测试时通过种群搜索（population search）和锦标赛选择（tournament selection）策略从候选证明中筛选出最佳结果。

Result: M3 模型在 MaxProof 框架加持下，在 IMO 2025 取得 35/42 分，在 USAMO 2026 取得 36/42 分，均超过了人类金牌录取分数线。

Conclusion: MaxProof 框架通过结合种群规模的测试时扩展（test-time scaling）与多维度模型能力，成功实现了在顶尖数学竞赛水平上的性能突破，证明了通过大规模验证与搜索机制可以显著提升语言模型的推理能力。

Abstract: We present MaxProof, a population-level test-time scaling framework for competition-level mathematical proof in the MiniMax-M3 series. M3 first trains three proof-oriented capabilities -- proof generation, proof verification, and critique-conditioned proof repair -- using a defense-in-depth generative verifier engineered for low false-positive rate. These capabilities are merged into a single released M3 model. At test time, MaxProof treats the model as a generator, verifier, refiner, and ranker, searches over a population of candidate proofs, and returns one final proof through tournament selection. With MaxProof test-time scaling, the M3 model reaches 35/42 on IMO 2025 and 36/42 on USAMO 2026, exceeding the human gold-medal threshold on both.

</details>


### [247] [WHAR Arena: Benchmarking the State of the Art in Efficient Wearable Human Activity Recognition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13194)
*Maximilian Burzer,Tobias King,Till Riedel,Michael Beigl,Tobias Röddiger*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对可穿戴人体活动识别领域评估不统一的问题，本文通过大规模基准测试证明现有模型预测性能已触及瓶颈，建议研究重心转向提升部署效率和模型鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前WHAR领域存在严重的“可比性危机”，即由于数据集、数据处理方式和评估协议不一致，导致现有研究的性能声明缺乏可靠性。

Method: 构建了一个包含30个多样化数据集的大规模开源基准测试框架，采用统一的数据处理、模型接口和跨主体评估协议；对17种代表性架构进行了4760次训练，并同步评估了预测性能与Android设备上的部署成本（延迟、峰值内存、模型大小）。

Result: 没有单一的架构能够统治该领域；当前主流架构的预测性能已趋于收敛。在考虑部署效率时，像TinierHAR这样的轻量级模型和传统的随机森林算法构成了帕累托最优前沿，而大型递归和混合模型往往以高昂的硬件成本换取微小的性能提升。

Conclusion: 可穿戴设备人体活动识别（WHAR）领域的预测性能已趋于饱和。未来的研究重心应从单纯追求精度转向优化部署效率（如模型轻量化）以及提高对领域偏移（domain shifts）的适应能力。

Abstract: Deep learning has become the dominant paradigm in Wearable Human Activity Recognition (WHAR), yet progress is obscured by a comparability crisis. Results are often reported using inconsistent datasets, custom data processing, and varying evaluation protocols, making state-of-the-art claims fragile. We address this with a large-scale, open-source benchmark that integrates 30 diverse datasets under standardized processing, unified model interfaces, and a shared cross-subject evaluation protocol. Evaluating 17 representative architectures across 4760 training runs, we jointly measure predictive performance alongside on-device latency, peak memory, and model size on an Android reference device. Our results reveal that the WHAR state of the art is distributed rather than dominated by a single architecture. While CNN-HAR achieves the highest mean macro-F1, top-performing models cluster tightly, indicating contemporary architectures have converged near a predictive performance ceiling. When accounting for deployment efficiency, compact neural models, such as TinierHAR, and classical Random Forests define the practically relevant Pareto frontier, whereas larger recurrent and hybrid models incur high hardware costs without corresponding performance gains. Consequently, while predictive performance has plateaued, substantial potential for future progress remains in optimizing deployment efficiency and improving adaptation to domain shifts. We release our full framework to support transparent reuse and extension.

### [248] [SupraBench: A Benchmark for Supramolecular Chemistry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13477)
*Tianyi Ma,Yijun Ma,Zehong Wang,Weixiang Sun,Ziming Li,Connor R. Schmidt,Chuxu Zhang,Matthew J. Webber,Yanfang Ye*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超分子化学中主客体系统的设计过程耗时，目前虽有大语言模型（LLM）应用于分子结合任务，但缺乏针对超分子领域逻辑推理（如亲和力预测）的系统性基准测试，限制了模型在该领域的开发与验证。

Method: 本文构建了首个超分子化学基准测试集SupraBench，包含绑定亲和力预测、最佳结合物选择、溶剂识别、描述任务及分子识别等五个维度；并发布了从Europe PMC整理的16M token超分子专用语料库SupraPMC，通过在不同开源和闭源LLM上进行领域自适应预训练与基准测试，评估其推理性能。

Result: 实验表明，主流大模型在SupraBench各任务中仍有较大改进空间；使用SupraPMC进行领域自适应预训练能显著提升模型在分布内回归任务的性能，但会导致模型在严格输出格式方面的表现下降；此外，不同任务类型的难度分布差异揭示了模型在化学逻辑推理方面的特定失败模式。

Conclusion: 本文通过发布SupraBench和SupraPMC，为超分子化学领域的LLM评估提供了基准和训练资源。研究表明，尽管大模型在相关任务上展现了一定潜力，但在复杂的超分子推理任务中仍面临巨大挑战，领域适应预训练在提升回归任务性能的同时可能牺牲输出格式的规范性，揭示了当前模型在跨模态推理和专业化学知识理解上的明确局限。

Abstract: Supramolecular chemistry, which includes the study of non-covalent host-guest assemblies, has advanced various applications. However, designing host-guest systems remains time-consuming, requiring days of dry-lab verification per candidate pair. Although LLMs have emerged as a fast alternative with strong performance on molecular binding tasks, no benchmark currently systematically evaluates LLMs for host-guest reasoning across fundamental supramolecular chemistry tasks, e.g., binding affinity prediction. To this end, we collaborate with domain experts to release the first Supramolecular Benchmark, called SupraBench, to evaluate LLMs in chemistry reasoning. Specifically, we design four fundamental tasks, i.e., binding affinity prediction, top-binder selection, solvent identification, and host-guest description, plus an auxiliary vision-based task for molecular identification. We also release SupraPMC, a curated 16M-token corpus of Supramolecular chemistry articles distilled from Europe PMC, to support the adaptation to the supramolecular domain. We benchmark a broad range of open and proprietary LLMs and find that LLMs leave substantial headroom across all tasks. Domain adaptation pretraining over SupraPMC transfers cleanly to in-distribution regression but trades off against strict letter-format output. Moreover, the difficulty profile differs sharply across task families, revealing distinct failure modes that indicate specific gaps in current supramolecular chemistry reasoning. Our source codes and benchmark datasets are available at https://github.com/Tianyi-Billy-Ma/SupraBench.

### [249] [From Uncertain Judgments to Calibrated Rankings: Conformal Elo Estimation for LLM Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13221)
*Bora Kargi,David Salinas*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究针对“LLM-as-a-judge”评估中的系统性偏差，提出了一种SoftElo方法，通过概率建模和保形预测，在无需大量人工介入的情况下，实现了与人类评估高度一致且具备不确定性校准的模型排名。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统大模型评估依赖昂贵的人工标注。虽然“LLM-as-a-judge”是一种更经济的替代方案，但现有的评判模型存在位置偏见、自我偏好和传递性错误等系统性问题，导致模型排名失真，亟需一种低成本且校准准确的自动评估方法。

Method: 该研究在两个层面解决了评估偏差问题：1. 局部层面：通过传播校准后的胜率（而非硬标签）进入Bradley-Terry模型，以处理judge的评分不确定性；2. 全局层面：应用分裂保形预测（Split Conformal Prediction）来量化LLM评分与人类评估之间的残差，从而生成具备边缘覆盖保证的预测区间。

Result: 实验表明，该方法显著提升了Elo估计的准确性，在LMArena的55个模型测试中，其推导的评分与人类评分的平均绝对误差（MAE）仅相差17.9 Elo，且该方法能够为开发者提供具有统计意义的置信区间。

Conclusion: 通过引入基于概率的评分和保形预测，该研究提出了一种高效、可靠的评估框架（SoftElo），能够在无需大规模人工标注的情况下，为大语言模型提供校准后的Elo评分及客观的不确定性界限，从而克服了现有“LLM-as-a-judge”评估方法中存在的系统性偏差。

Abstract: Evaluating new large language models typically requires costly human annotation campaigns at scale. LLM-as-a-judge offers a cheaper alternative, but judge scores carry systematic errors - such as position bias, self-preference, or intransitivity - that can strongly miscalibrate the resulting rankings. We quantify the resulting judge-human disagreement at two complementary levels. At the local level, we estimate per-battle uncertainty from the judge's own score differences by propagating calibrated win probabilities rather than hard labels into the Bradley-Terry procedure. This alone provides a drastic improvement to Elo estimation accuracy, bringing LLM-derived ratings within 17.9 Elo MAE of human-derived ones when averaged over 55 held-out models on LMArena. At the global level, we apply split conformal prediction to the residual gap between LLM-derived and human-derived Elo ratings across held-out models, producing prediction intervals with distribution-free marginal coverage guarantees that account for irreducible LLM-human disagreement. Together, these two layers yield a low-cost evaluation tool that provides developers with calibrated Elo estimates and honest uncertainty bounds, without access to large-scale human annotations.To facilitate reproducibility, we release our code at https://github.com/kargibora/SoftElo .

</details>


### [250] [Distributional Loss for Robust Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13223)
*Kathleen Anderson,Thomas Martinetz*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的监督学习通常采用硬标签（One-hot）映射，忽略了样本本身的类别歧义，容易导致过拟合，且在数据受限的情况下难以学习到稳健的决策边界。

Method: 提出了一种新的损失函数概念，不再将输入样本直接映射为单一标签，而是将分类器的输出分布目标定义为双峰高斯分布，从而在训练过程中引入对类别模糊性的建模。

Result: 实验结果表明，该方法能够一致性地提升分类模型的鲁棒性，特别是在小样本（low-data）场景下表现突出，且对现有训练流程的改动极小。

Conclusion: 该论文提出了一种基于双峰高斯分布的软标签优化方法，通过隐式建模类别模糊性，在不增加额外标注的前提下，显著提升了分类模型在小样本环境下的鲁棒性和泛化性能。

Abstract: This paper proposes a novel loss concept for supervised classification tasks. Rather than enforcing a direct mapping from each input sample to a single assigned label, we define an optimization objective over all classifier outputs as a bimodal Gaussian distribution. This softer target formulation implicitly captures class ambiguity, mitigates overfitting, and encourages the learning of more robust decision boundaries, all without requiring additional label information. Experimental results demonstrate consistent improvements in robustness, with particularly pronounced gains in low-data regimes, while requiring only minimal modifications to standard training pipelines.

### [251] [Beyond the Commitment Boundary: Probing Epiphenomenal Chain-of-Thought in Large Reasoning Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13603)
*Daniel Scalena,Sara Candussio,Luca Bortolussi,Elisabetta Fersini,Malvina Nissim,Gabriele Sarti*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究发现语言模型的思维链存在“承诺边界”，在此之后的大部分推理步骤是冗余的。通过识别并剔除这些冗余步骤，可以在保证模型性能的前提下，将推理链长度平均缩减 55%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管思维链（CoT）是目前大语言模型推理的主流范式，但学术界对其内部推理步骤如何真正影响最终答案的因果关系缺乏深入理解，且现有的CoT推理效率较低。

Method: 作者通过“早期退出”（early exit）机制来评估推理过程中每一步对最终答案的因果重要性，并利用注意力探针（attention probes）分析推理链中答案形成的阶段，通过识别“承诺边界”实现推理步数的动态缩减。

Result: 研究发现推理过程中存在一个明显的“承诺边界”，即模型在推理链中途会迅速从不确定的中间状态转变为高置信度的最终答案状态，随后的大部分推理步骤对结果没有实际影响（即附带现象）。利用此机制可将思维链长度平均缩减 55%，且对模型性能的影响微乎其微。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了语言模型推理过程中的“承诺边界”现象，证明了推理链中大部分步骤在确定最终答案后是冗余的。通过识别这一边界并进行早期退出，可以在几乎不损失模型性能的前提下大幅提升推理效率。

Abstract: Chain-of-thought (CoT) reasoning is the dominant paradigm for inference-time scaling in language models, yet the causal influence of individual steps on the final answer poorly understood. We estimate each step's causal importance via early exit and use this measure to study how answers form across the reasoning traces of several model families. Across diverse tasks, we find that reasoning typically crosses a \emph{commitment boundary} -- a sharp transition from transient intermediate guesses to a stable, high-confidence answer. This transition often happens in a single step, well before the model's reasoning block ends, and is followed by \emph{epiphenomenal} CoT steps that leave the final answer probability unaltered. Using attention probes, we show that answer-formation stages can be linearly decoded from intermediate reasoning steps with high accuracy and generalize robustly to unseen reasoning tasks. We exploit this signal to early-exit reasoning blocks at the commitment boundary, reducing the length of CoTs up to 55\% on average with negligible impact on model performance.

</details>


### [252] [ReSET: Accurate Latency-Critical NVFP4 Reasoning via Step-Aware Temperature Scaling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13233)
*Sihwa Lee,Janghwan Lee,Donghoon Yoo,Jae Gon Kim,Hanyul Ryu,Soojung Ryu,Jungwook Choi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对大模型在 NVFP4 量化推理中的精度下降与延迟瓶颈，本文提出了 ReSET 方法。通过动态温度缩放策略补偿量化带来的不确定性，并配合优化的 CUDA 内核，在显著提升解码速度的同时改善了推理准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大推理模型（LRM）提升了复杂问题解决能力，但推理成本高昂。NVFP4 量化虽能降低成本，但直接应用会导致推理精度下降，且现有的 NVFP4 内核在小批量自回归解码中无法充分体现性能优势。因此需要一种既能保持精度又能降低延迟的优化方案。

Method: 1. 分析量化对推理过程中 token 级不确定性的影响，发现量化会导致低熵符号标记的错误采样及高不确定性步骤中的标记过度集中。
2. 提出 ReSET (Reasoning-step Entropy-based Temperature-scaling)：一种基于推理步骤熵的在线温度缩放方法，利用 token 级和步骤级熵信号动态调整解码温度。
3. 设计了针对小批量自回归解码的 CUDA-core small-M NVFP4 内核，专门优化延迟敏感场景。

Result: 1. 在多个推理基准测试中，ReSET 相比原始 NVFP4 基准提升了约 2 个点的推理准确率。
2. 新设计的 CUDA 内核在 kernel 级别实现了相比 vLLM NVFP4 高达 2.5 倍的加速。
3. 在端到端的解码过程中，相比 BF16 精度模型实现了约 2 倍的推理速度提升。

Conclusion: ReSET 成功解决了 NVFP4 量化在大模型推理中的精度损失和延迟瓶颈问题。通过结合推理步骤的熵分析与专门优化的 CUDA 内核，该方法在保持推理精度的同时，显著提升了推理效率，为低精度大模型推理提供了高效的落地方案。

Abstract: Large reasoning models (LRMs) improve complex problem-solving by generating long intermediate reasoning traces, but this substantially increases inference costs. NVFP4 inference offers a promising approach to reduce both computational and memory costs through hardware-supported low-precision execution. However, directly applying NVFP4 to LRMs introduces two practical limitations: reasoning accuracy degrades under quantization, and existing NVFP4 kernels do not fully realize latency benefits in small-batch autoregressive decoding. In this work, we analyze the effect of NVFP4 quantization on token-level uncertainty during reasoning. We show that quantization increases incorrect sampling at low-entropy symbolic tokens, while causing over-concentration on a small set of tokens in high-uncertainty reasoning steps. Based on this observation, we propose \textbf{ReSET}, a reasoning-step entropy-based temperature-scaling method that estimates step-level uncertainty online and adapts the decoding temperature using both token-level and step-level entropy signals. To address the latency gap, we further design a CUDA-core small-$M$ NVFP4 kernel for latency-critical autoregressive decoding. Across reasoning benchmarks and model scales, ReSET improves NVFP4 reasoning accuracy by up to $\sim\!$2 points over the NVFP4 baseline. Our CUDA-core small-$M$ kernel further improves latency-critical decoding, delivering up to $2.5\!\times$ kernel-level speedup over NVFP4 vLLM and approximately $2\!\times$ end-to-end decoding speedup over BF16. Code is available at https://github.com/aiha-lab/ReSET.

</details>

*Olga Isupova,Danil Kuzin,Ella Browning,Tom Mills,Steven Reece*

Abstract: Passive acoustic monitoring holds great promise for ecological inference, yet existing automated tools are typically narrowly trained and non-transferable. We address these limitations with PULSE, a semi-supervised, multi-task framework for Orthoptera bioacoustics, combining weakly-supervised species classification, self-supervised learning on unlabelled field audio, and knowledge distillation from a general-purpose bioacoustic model. Our domain-adapted specialist model outperforms a state-of-the-art general model across all metrics (macro F1: 0.21 vs. 0.07; AUC: 0.74 vs. 0.45; AP: 0.32 vs. 0.19), with active learning further raising F1 to 0.34 and AUC to 0.84. ### [254] [Towards More General Control of Diffusion Models Using Jeffrey Guidance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13240)
*Raphaël Razafindralambo,Rémy Sun,Frédéric Precioso,Jes Frellsen,Pierre-Alexandre Mattei*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于Jeffrey条件化规则的扩散模型引导框架（Jeffrey guidance），通过对分布进行最小化扰动，有效提升了模型采样过程的可控性，并在图像质量优化与属性公平性约束任务中取得了优异效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的扩散模型引导技术（如分类器引导）多依赖于启发式的采样规则或隐式的能量函数，难以处理更复杂、非显式的分布控制需求。作者旨在通过建立一个更具原则性的统计框架，实现对扩散模型输出的更精细、更具普适性的控制。

Method: 作者提出了“Jeffrey引导”（Jeffrey guidance），利用概率论中的Jeffrey条件化规则（Jeffrey's rule of conditioning）来调整扩散模型的边缘分布。该方法通过引入目标分布约束，在保持原模型条件结构的同时，对生成样本进行最小化扰动，从而引导采样过程向预设目标靠拢。

Result: 实验表明，在CIFAR-10和FFHQ数据集上，使用Jeffrey引导调整Inception嵌入分布能显著降低FID分数，提升图像质量；此外，该方法在CelebA-HQ数据集上成功实现了对特定属性的公平性约束（强制属性独立）。

Conclusion: Jeffrey引导提供了一种基于统计学原理的控制框架，它通过最小化对原始联合分布的扰动，有效地实现了对扩散模型生成分布的精确重定向，为图像生成中的质量提升和属性约束（如公平性）提供了鲁棒的理论与实践工具。

Abstract: A key strength of diffusion models lies in their flexibility, since their outputs can be controlled at sampling time through guidance. However, beyond simple cases such as conditional sampling, the target distribution is often left implicit, defined only through a sampling rule or a heuristic energy function. To address this, we propose Jeffrey guidance, a principled framework that extends diffusion-model control to applications beyond what standard guidance can express. It leverages Jeffrey's rule of conditioning to update marginal distributions towards a prescribed target, preserving the conditional structure and minimally perturbing the joint distribution. We first demonstrate Jeffrey guidance by targeting a prescribed embedding distribution. With Inception embeddings as the target, this leads to substantial reductions in FID on both CIFAR-10 and FFHQ. We further apply Jeffrey guidance to fairness on CelebA-HQ, updating an unconditional diffusion model to enforce independence between attributes.

</details>

### [256] [Extracting Governing Equations from Latent Dynamics via Multi-View Contrastive Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13260)
*Paolo Muratore,Mackenzie Weygandt Mathis*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从含噪的高维测量数据中识别潜在动力系统是表示学习、系统辨识及科学发现领域的关键挑战。现有方法在处理非线性观测噪声和保证可识别性方面存在局限，研究旨在解决这些现实场景下的动力系统建模难题。

Method: 提出了一种多视角时间对比学习算法（DYSCO），通过利用同一动力过程的多个独立且含噪的视角来解耦信号与噪声。同时，该方法将动力学参数化为结构化函数基，支持在仿射规范内进行控制方程的符号化恢复。

Result: 实验表明，DYSCO在多种动力学体系（如混沌、振荡和亚稳态）下，均能准确恢复潜在轨迹和流场，且在处理高斯噪声及神经记录中常见的泊松噪声时均表现出优异的鲁棒性。

Abstract: Identifying latent dynamical systems from noisy, high-dimensional measurements is a central problem at the intersection of representation learning, system identification, and scientific discovery. We present DYSCO, a multi-view temporal contrastive learning algorithm that jointly recovers latent trajectories and the governing dynamics from such observations, by leveraging multiple independent noisy views of the same underlying process to disentangle signal from noise. By parameterizing the dynamics in a structured functional basis, our framework further enables symbolic recovery of the governing equations within an affine gauge. We offer theoretical guarantees for strong identification up to an affine indeterminacy, extending prior identifiability results to the realistic setting of noisy nonlinear observations. Empirically, we demonstrate accurate recovery of both latent trajectories and flow fields across a diverse set of dynamical regimes (e.g., chaotic, oscillatory, and metastable) under both Gaussian and Poisson observation noise, the latter being particularly relevant for neural recordings.

### [257] [Different Layers, Different Manifolds: Module-Wise Weight-Space Geometry in Transformer Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13276)
*Kirato Yoshihara*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究揭示了Transformer优化中模块特定的几何重要性：通过对Attention层施加Stiefel约束、MLP层施加DGram约束，可有效避免训练不稳定性并显著提升模型性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的深度学习优化通常对所有权重矩阵应用统一的流形约束，忽略了Transformer中不同层（Attention与MLP）在几何空间上的差异化偏好，导致优化效率受限。

Method: 研究引入了“Manifold Muon”方法，针对GPT-2预训练任务，对Attention块和MLP块分别尝试配置Stiefel和DGram流形约束，并比较了不同模块间约束分配的组合效果，同时分析了权重矩阵奇异值增长对训练稳定性的影响。

Result: 实验发现存在明显的几何不对称性：将Stiefel约束用于Attention层、DGram约束用于MLP层表现最优。相反，若将配置反转或全部使用DGram，在共享超参数下会导致训练不稳定；原因在于DGram约束在Attention层会导致奇异值增长，引起Attention Logits过大及Softmax饱和。

Conclusion: 针对Transformer模型的优化不应采用统一的几何约束，而应根据不同模块（Attention与MLP）的特性实施特定的几何约束（如Attention使用Stiefel流形，MLP使用DGram流形），从而提升训练的稳定性与性能。

Abstract: Weight-space geometry plays a central role in neural network optimization, yet manifold constraints are often applied uniformly across all weight matrices. In this work, we ask whether different transformer modules prefer different manifold geometries. We study Manifold Muon for GPT-2 pretraining and compare layer-wise assignments of Stiefel and DGram constraints across attention and MLP blocks. Our results show a clear asymmetry: constraining attention layers with Stiefel geometry while assigning DGram geometry to MLP layers gives the best performance among the tested configurations, whereas the inverted assignment and all-DGram configuration become unstable under the shared hyperparameter setting. We trace this failure to singular value growth in DGram-constrained attention weights, which can amplify attention logits and induce softmax saturation. These findings suggest that symmetry-aware and geometry-aware optimization for transformers should be module-specific rather than uniform.

### [258] [Once-for-All: Scalable Simultaneous Forecasting via Equilibrium State Estimation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13285)
*Beinan Xu,Andy Song,Jiti Gao,Feng Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为平衡状态估计（ESE）的预测范式，通过在单次传递中预测所有相互作用的系统，实现了比现有方法快 10-70 倍的预测速度，同时保证了高精度、良好的鲁棒性和线性扩展能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实世界中存在大量需要同时预测多个相互作用系统（如经济、医疗建模）的场景，现有逐一预测方法在计算效率和多系统扩展性上存在瓶颈。

Method: 提出平衡状态估计（Equilibrium State Estimation, ESE）范式。该方法首先跨系统估计平衡状态，随后基于当前状态与平衡状态的偏差进行整体预测。该模型具有线性时间复杂度，并可与现有的预测模型无缝集成。

Result: 实验表明，ESE 在合成及真实数据集（如货币汇率、COVID-19 传播）上表现出色，精度不亚于现有最先进方法（SOTA），同时在计算速度上实现了 10-70 倍的提升，并展现出良好的稳健性与可扩展性。

Conclusion: ESE 是一种高效、可扩展且稳健的协同预测框架，通过引入平衡状态估计，成功解决了多系统协同预测的计算效率和扩展性问题，在保持预测精度的同时大幅提升了计算速度，具有广泛的应用前景。

Abstract: We introduce Equilibrium State Estimation (ESE), a novel paradigm for simultaneous prediction, where multiple interacting systems require separate yet coordinated forecasts. Such scenarios often arise in real-world settings such as economics and healthcare modeling. Unlike existing approaches that predict one system at a time, ESE forecasts all systems in a single pass. It first estimates the equilibrium state across systems, then generates holistic forecasts based on the difference between the current state and the estimated equilibrium. Extensive experiments on synthetic and real-world datasets, including currency exchange and COVID-19 spread modeling, demonstrate that ESE is at least as accurate as state-of-the-art (SOTA) methods while being significantly faster. In addition, ESE integrates seamlessly with conventional predictors, combining their accuracy with its exceptional efficiency and delivering a 10-70x speedup. With linear-time complexity, ESE scales far better than SOTA methods as the number of systems increases. Moreover, it remains accurate under diverse perturbations, establishing ESE as a fast, generalizable, robust, and scalable multi-prediction method.

### [259] [Clipping Makes Distributed and Federated Asynchronous SGD Robust to Stragglers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13287)
*Samuel Erickson,Mikael Johansson*

TL;DR: 本文从理论上证实了梯度裁剪能够消除异步随机梯度下降中延迟对收敛速度的负面影响，并利用更广泛的子Weibull噪声模型证明了算法在高概率下的收敛性。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究采用了基于子Weibull（sub-Weibull）分布的梯度噪声模型，该模型能够更全面地刻画深度学习中常见的重尾噪声特征；通过数学分析推导了梯度裁剪在异步随机梯度下降（ASGD）中的作用，并证明了算法的期望收敛性以及首次提供了异步优化中的高概率收敛性证明。

Result: 理论分析表明，引入梯度裁剪后，异步随机梯度下降的预言机复杂度（oracle complexity）不再依赖于最大延迟；此外，研究还证明了该算法在子Weibull噪声假设下不仅能够达到期望收敛，还能实现高概率收敛。

Conclusion: 本文首次在异步优化领域证明了梯度裁剪在处理异步延迟方面的理论优势，通过理论分析证实了梯度裁剪能够消除收敛速度对最大延迟的依赖，从而在存在重尾梯度噪声的环境下显著增强了异步随机梯度下降算法的稳定性和收敛性能。

Abstract: In modern machine learning, parallelization of training is an important strategy for increasing scale. Asynchronous stochastic gradient descent (ASGD), which maximizes the utilization of available hardware by avoiding waiting for slow workers. However, with constant step sizes, the convergence of ASGD is nonetheless affected negatively by slow workers due to large delays in updates. At the same time, it has been empirically observed in asynchronous training of deep learning models that gradient clipping "stabilizes" training. In this work, we provide a theoretical justification for this behavior, as we show that clipping removes the dependence of the maximum delay in the oracle complexity. We employ a sub-Weibull model of gradient noise which generalizes sub-Gaussian and sub-exponential distributions to more heavy-tailed distributions, motivated by empirical observations in deep learning. We show convergence in expectation, and the first time in asynchronous optimization, convergence with high probability.

### [260] [Quantizing Time-Series Models As Dynamical Systems: Trajectory-Based Quantization Sensitivity Score](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13300)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的后训练量化（PTQ）方法通常将敏感度分析与量化过程紧密耦合，难以应对黑盒模型或已融合算子的网络，且往往依赖于繁琐的校准数据或计算密集的二阶导数估计。

Method: 1. 提出轨迹量化敏感度分数（TQS）：将神经网络的推理过程建模为离散时间动力系统，通过量化误差在滚动时域内的传播与放大来衡量其敏感度。

Abstract: We introduce the Trajectory-based Quantization Sensitivity Score (TQS), a metric that reframes post-training quantization (PTQ) through the lens of dynamical-systems stability. By modeling the network's rollout as a discrete-time dynamical system, TQS characterizes how quantization-induced errors propagate and amplify over the rollout horizon. Unlike conventional PTQ methods, where sensitivity analysis is often coupled to the quantization procedure, TQS enables a priori sensitivity estimation decoupled from quantizer selection and bit-width assignment. This separation allows for quantization budget planning even for black-box or compiled networks with fused operators. Building on this, we present TQS-PTQ, a flexible mixed-precision framework that requires no calibration data or costly second-order approximations. Our experiments show that a dynamical-systems perspective provides a robust, high-performing pathway for low-precision deployment in resource-constrained settings.

### [261] [Rarity-Gated Context Conditioning for Offline Imitation Learning-Based Maritime Anomaly Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13311)
*Yongmin Kim,ByeongHoon Jeon,Sungil Kim*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对上下文分布不平衡导致的异常检测误报问题，该论文提出了一种基于稀有度感知门控的特征调制模块（RGFiLM），能够根据上下文的频率动态调整调制强度，从而显著提升了异常检测的鲁棒性和准确性。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种名为“稀有度门控特征线性调制”（RGFiLM）的新颖模块。该方法结合了特征级调制（通过缩放和移位调整隐藏特征）与数据驱动的稀有度评分门控机制。稀有度评分基于上下文变量的经验分布计算得出，在罕见上下文中增强调制强度，在频繁上下文中保持保守，从而缓解了频率偏差导致的决策不稳定问题。

Result: 在海上船舶轨迹异常检测任务的实验中，RGFiLM 相比于现有的上下文无关和上下文条件方法，在平均 F1 分数与误报率（FPR）之间取得了最优的权衡，验证了其在处理环境敏感数据时的有效性。

Abstract: Contextual anomaly detection aims to identify abnormal behavior conditional on context variables, but practical deployments often face highly imbalanced context distributions where rare regimes can be critical information. Under such frequency bias, context-conditioned models can produce unstable decisions and excessive false alarms in rare contexts. We propose Rarity-Gated Feature-wise Linear Modulation (RGFiLM), a rarity-aware conditioning module that combines feature-wise modulation (i.e., context-conditioned scaling and shifting of hidden features) with a gate controlled by a data-driven rarity score. The rarity score is estimated from the empirical distribution of context variables and regulates how strongly context modulates intermediate representations: the gate becomes more decisive under rare contexts while remaining conservative under frequent contexts. We evaluate RGFiLM on maritime trajectory anomaly detection using AIS motion sequences with ERA5 environmental context in an environment-sensitive detour scenario. When instantiated in a sequential anomaly scoring pipeline, RGFiLM achieves the best mean F1--False Positive Rate (FPR) trade-off among the compared context-agnostic and context-conditioned methods. These results suggest that explicitly accounting for context rarity is an effective approach for reducing false alarms in context-sensitive anomaly detection.

### [262] [Navigating the Safety-Fidelity Trade-off: Massive-Variate Time Series Forecasting for Power Systems via Probabilistic Scenarios](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13338)
*Kaijie Xu,Anqi Wang,Xilin Dai*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了针对大规模电力传输网的概率预测基准PowerPhase，并设计了PowerForge模型，旨在解决高维物理系统中概率分布精度与物理约束满足度之间的权衡难题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多元概率预测基准测试规模较小（不超过2,000个通道），且缺乏针对复杂物理系统（如输电网）的物理特性与操作约束的综合评估，无法满足工业级大规模系统的需求。

Method: 1. 构建了包含六个输电网、高达36,964个联合预测通道的PowerPhase大规模基准测试集；2. 引入了包括Safety_mBrier、NECV和CVaR-alpha在内的约束感知评估指标；3. 提出了PowerForge预测模型，该模型采用基于场景的分位数预测、类型特定的解码头以及变量组间的因果桥接机制。

Result: PowerPhase基准测试发现分布准确性与约束满足度之间存在显著的“安全-保真度”（safety-fidelity）权衡；PowerForge模型在所有测试电网中均取得了最佳的平均排名，验证了其在大规模、受限物理系统预测任务中的有效性。

Conclusion: 本文通过引入PowerPhase基准测试，揭示了多元概率预测在复杂物理系统（如输电网）中分布准确性与约束满足度之间的“安全-保真度”权衡，并证明了PowerForge模型在处理大规模高维度物理约束系统时的优越性。

Abstract: Probabilistic forecasting models are increasingly deployed on multivariate systems with distinct channel physics and operational constraints, but existing benchmarks evaluate neither property at scale. Public canonical multivariate benchmarks cap out at 2,000 channels, while power-system benchmarks either lack temporal structure or probabilistic evaluation. We introduce PowerPhase, a probabilistic forecasting benchmark built on six transmission grids ranging from 2,000 to 36,964 jointly forecasted channels, more than an order of magnitude beyond popular canonical multivariate benchmarks. Each target trajectory is the output of an AC power-flow solve, and PowerPhase ships with constraint-aware metrics, including Safety_mBrier, NECV, and CVaR-alpha, that complement CRPS and Distortion. Across eight baselines and three seeds, distributional accuracy and constraint satisfaction rank models differently, a trade-off we term safety-fidelity. We further propose PowerForge, a scenario-based quantile forecaster with type-specific decoding heads and a causal bridge between variable groups, which achieves the best average rank on every grid.

</details>


### [263] [Enhanced Low-Density Region Exploration in Classifier-Guided Diffusion Models Through Modified Reverse Diffusion Sampling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13347)
*Jagriti Singh,Shekhar Verma,Muneendra Ojha*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种无需额外训练的扩散模型采样优化方法，通过在采样过程中引入针对低密度区域的梯度引导和真实图像引导，有效提升了模型对长尾稀有样本的覆盖能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于分类器引导的扩散模型倾向于生成高密度区域的样本，导致长尾分布中的稀有样本覆盖率不足；而现有的改进方案通常需要额外的网络训练或资源消耗。因此，研究旨在寻求一种无需额外训练、能有效改善长尾样本覆盖的采样策略。

Method: 在预训练的条件扩散模型基础上，作者引入了两种新的采样时引导策略：1. 修改分类器梯度，将采样轨迹引导至低置信度（低密度）区域；2. 在每一步采样中加入向预测真实图像的引导，以确保生成的样本位于真实数据流形上。该方法无需额外模型训练。

Result: 在ImageNet数据集上的实验表明，该方法在64x64分辨率下提升了ADM模型的召回率（Recall），同时保持了相当的FID分数；在256x256分辨率下，通过组合不同的引导策略，验证了生成样本的视觉多样性和感知质量。

Conclusion: 该研究提出了一种无需额外训练的采样时间密度感知引导方法，通过调整分类器梯度和预测图像引导，有效提升了扩散模型在长尾分布下的样本覆盖率与多样性。

Abstract: Diffusion models have emerged as state-of-the-art generative models for high-fidelity image synthesis, particularly in their classifier-free guided and classifier-guided forms. However, standard classifier guidance concentrates probability mass around high-density class mean, leading to poor coverage of rare samples in the tails of the class-conditional distributions. Recent work on diffusion-based tail sampling mitigates this by training an additional low-density-seeking classifier with a synthetic-vs-real discriminator, at the cost of additional networks and training. In parallel, a number of samplers and distillation techniques accelerate or refine diffusion sampling, but do not explicitly address long-tail coverage. We propose a purely sampling-time, density-aware extension of classifier-guided conditional diffusion model that targets low-density regions without any additional training. We have applied guidance at noisy images not on predicted noise like most diffusion models. Starting from a pretrained conditional diffusion model and classifier on ImageNet, we modify the guided reverse dynamics by steering trajectories toward low-confidence regions via the modified classifier gradient, and at each time step, we also guide the sampling process toward the predicted real image. 1st guidance helps explore low-probability samples, and 2nd guidance helps to generate samples to be close to the real data manifold. The proposed sampler consistently improves ADM model recall at 64x64 resolution while maintaining a comparable FID, and with a 256x256 ADM model, we showed the results visually with different combinations of both guidance. We also showed that standard ADM classifier guidance, combined with predicted real image guidance, helps generate high perceptual quality samples with a 256x256 ADM model on ImageNet.

### [264] [VideoMDM: Towards 3D Human Motion Generation From 2D Supervision](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13364)
*Amir Mann,Gal Michael Harari,Merav Keidar,Or Litany*

Main category: cs.LG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的高质量3D人体运动数据获取成本高昂且规模有限，而单目视频数据极其丰富。如何摆脱对3D真值（Ground Truth）的依赖，直接从2D视频中学习生成3D人体运动模型成为研究重点。

Method: 提出了一种基于扩散模型的框架VideoMDM。通过预训练的2D转3D提升器提供初始的“噪声老师”预测；在训练过程中，模型在3D空间执行去噪，并通过将预测重投影回2D与原始视频关键点对比来进行监督；同时引入了深度加权的2D重投影损失及速度一致性和过参数化表示对齐等运动正则化手段。

Result: 在HumanML3D数据集上，VideoMDM的生成质量（FID 0.88）非常接近完全基于3D监督的模型（FID 0.54）；在Fit3D和NBA等真实视频数据集上，生成的运动表现出极高的真实感，且在人类主观评价中具有显著优势。

Conclusion: VideoMDM证明了在没有3D真值监督的情况下，仅利用单目视频的2D关键点也可以学习到高质量的3D人体运动先验。该方法通过将2D重投影损失与3D运动正则化相结合，有效弥补了监督信号的缺失，为从海量视频数据中学习3D运动提供了新的范式。

Abstract: We introduce VideoMDM, a diffusion-based framework that trains 3D human motion priors directly from accurate 2D poses extracted from monocular videos, without any 3D ground truth. A pretrained 2D-to-3D lifter provides approximate 3D pose sequences that serve as a noisy teacher: these are diffused, denoised by the model in 3D, and supervised in 2D by reprojecting the prediction and comparing against accurate keypoints. We show that, under mild assumptions, a depth-weighted 2D reprojection loss is equivalent in expectation to direct 3D supervision, and we adapt standard 3D motion regularizers - velocity consistency and over-parameterized representation alignment - to this 2D setting. Unlike methods that lift 2D to 3D only at inference, VideoMDM learns a coherent 3D motion manifold during training. On HumanML3D it nearly closes the gap to fully 3D-supervised MDM (FID 0.88 vs 0.54); On real video datasets Fit3D and NBA the method learns to generate motions consistently preferred by humans, with strong quantitative results.

### [265] [Positional Encoding in the Context of Memristor-Based Analog Computation for Automatic Speech Recognition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13379)
*Benedikt Hilmes,Nick Rossenbach,Ralf Schlüter*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究解决了Transformer位置编码在大规模忆阻器神经网络计算中引发的ADC精度降级问题，通过调整ADC位宽配置或简化线性变换，显著提升了计算准确性，同时保持了能效比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 忆阻器在进行模拟向量-矩阵乘法计算时，因权重编程和执行过程中的物理失真导致计算误差。现有的忆阻器神经网络计算在处理Transformer模型中的特定变换（如位置编码）时存在较大的性能退化，限制了其在自然语言处理任务中的应用。

Method: 1. 识别并分析了Transformer模型中位置编码所产生的大数值输出对忆阻器模数转换器（ADC）造成的精度降级影响；2. 提出了通过调整特定层级的权重比例与ADC精度位宽的优化策略；3. 提出了一种在ADC硬件不可更改情况下的备选方案，即移除编码相关的线性变换层。

Result: 通过调整ADC配置，计算执行的性能降级相对减少了约50%，且保持了预期的能耗稳定性；在无法修改ADC的限制条件下，通过移除编码相关的线性变换，性能降级也可减少约30%。

Conclusion: 通过对忆阻器计算中位置编码转换引起的输出失真进行分析与优化，可以在不增加能耗的前提下显著提高计算精度。研究表明，针对特定层优化ADC配置或移除冗余的线性变换，是提升忆阻器神经网络计算性能的有效途径。

Abstract: Memristors provide a new chance for resource-efficient computation of neural models for natural language processing by enabling analog execution of vector-matrix-multiplication. Yet, computations on these devices are currently subject to larger distortion, both in weight programming and execution. In this work, we identify large output values of transformed positional encodings to cause major degradation within analog-to-digital conversion (ADC) as part of memristor-based computation. By adjusting the proportion of weight and precision bits of the ADC of specific memristor layers, we reduce the degradation of the execution by ~50% relative, while keeping the estimated energy consumption stable. Additionally, we investigate scenarios where the ADC cannot be modified. In that case the degradation can be reduced by ~30% relative after removing encoding-related linear transformations.

### [266] [Hölder++: Improving the Quality-Coherence Trade-off in Multimodal VAEs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13381)
*Huyen Vo,María Martínez-García,Isabel Valera*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多模态变分自编码器（VAEs）在生成质量（真实感、多样性）与一致性（模态间的语义关联）之间存在权衡。虽然基于 Hölder 池化的简单近似方法提升了一致性，但牺牲了样本多样性，研究旨在通过更优的架构设计解决这一平衡问题。

Method: 提出了 Hölder++ 模型：(1) 实现了无需近似的精确 Hölder 池化机制；(2) 采用共享与私有表示结合的架构 (Hölder+) 来解耦模态特征；(3) 引入分层推断 (Hierarchical Inference) 进一步增强共享与私有表示的解耦效果。

Result: 实验证明，Hölder++ 在维持高质量生成的同时，显著增强了跨模态一致性，产生了结构更清晰的潜在空间，并且学习到的共享表示对下游任务具有更强的表征能力。

Conclusion: Hölder++ 通过引入精确的 Hölder 池化、共享与私有表示建模以及分层推断机制，成功缓解了多模态 VAE 在生成质量与跨模态一致性之间的权衡难题。该方法不仅在生成性能上优于现有模型，还提升了潜在空间的结构化程度和下游任务的表现。

Abstract: Existing approaches for multimodal variational autoencoders (VAEs) face a trade-off between generative quality and coherence-i.e., they struggle to generate realistic and diverse samples that, at the same time, are semantically consistent across modalities. A recent work shows that using a simple approximation to Hölder pooling as an aggregation method improves coherence over the SOTA MMVAE+, despite assuming a single shared representation across all modalities. Yet, it slightly compromises sample diversity. Inspired by this insight, we propose Hölder++, a novel multimodal VAE that improves the generative quality-coherence trade-off through: (i) the first implementation of Hölder pooling without any approximation for multimodal VAEs; (ii) an extended architecture that models distinct shared and private (i.e., modality-specific) representations (Hölder+); and (iii) hierarchical inference that further enhances the disentanglement between the shared and private representations (Hölder++). Our experiments corroborate that Hölder++ consistently improves the generative quality-coherence trade-off, yields more structured latent spaces, and learns shared representations that are informative for downstream tasks.

### [267] [PolyFlow: Safe and Efficient Polytope-Constrained Flow Matching with Constraint Embedding and Projection-free Update](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13400)

Abstract: While flow-based generative models have demonstrated strong performance across a wide range of domains, deploying them in safety-critical physical systems remains challenging due to strict constraint requirements. Existing approaches typically enforce safety through post-hoc corrections, which incur substantial computational overhead and may distort the learned distribution. We propose PolyFlow, a polytope-constrained flow matching framework that embeds constraints directly into the model and flow dynamics. PolyFlow introduces a discrete-time flow formulation and a projection-free architecture, which eliminate the discretization error and guarantee strict satisfaction of arbitrary polyhedral constraints, without the need for expensive iterative solvers. Experimental results show that PolyFlow achieves zero constraint violation while maintaining high distributional fidelity across a range of planning and control tasks. Compared to state-of-the-art constrained generation baselines, PolyFlow significantly reduces inference latency and demonstrates a favorable trade-off between safety, efficiency, and generative quality. Code is available on https://github.com/MJianM/PolyFlow.

Abstract: Speculative decoding speeds up LLM inference by using a draft model to generate tokens, with an acceptance-rejection scheme that ensures that the output matches the target distribution. While straightforward in discrete spaces, efficiently sampling this residual in continuous space is non-trivial. Consequently, existing diffusion adaptations either use computationally inefficient sampling techniques or rely on an alternative scheme. In this work, we introduce a novel scheme that efficiently implements the original speculative sampling mechanism for diffusion models. Our approach offers a critical advantage over current methods: it enables us to adapt block verification from LLMs to diffusions -- which provably improves the acceptance rate of drafts. Abstract: Neural operators have emerged as a powerful data-driven approach for solving time-dependent PDEs. Our preliminary experiments reveal that optimal memory weight varies with resolution and viscosity, implying that a fixed memory weight cannot simultaneously optimize performance across diverse settings. We propose AMGFNO, which dynamically modulates memory weight through a learnable gate. On the Kuramoto-Sivashinsky and Burgers' equations, AMGFNO achieves 55-79% nRMSE reduction over at low resolution, with the learned gate value automatically decreasing from $\bar{g} \approx 0.7$ to near-zero as resolution increases.

### [270] [Clustering Node Attributed Networks with Graph Neural Networks and Self Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13444)

Abstract: Graph clustering - partitioning the node set of a graph into disjoint subsets that reflect some latent information - is a fundamental problem as it finds applications in a myriad of different scenarios. While this classic problem has been tackled for decades by different communities, a recent variation of the problem driven by real data considers the scenario where nodes have attributes that are also informative. This has triggered novel methods that simultaneously leverage network information (edges) and node information (attributed) in the design of novel clustering algorithms. This work proposes a novel framework that builds on prior works that have applied graph neural networks (GNN) to graph clustering. The proposed framework operates in rounds of self learning in a fully unsupervised setting. In each round, a GNN generates representations for nodes that are used to cluster the nodes. This clustering influences the graph used to generate the node representation in the next round. Moreover, a context graph built in each round using the original graph is used to generate the node representations. Empirical results show that the proposed methodology extracts information from both network edges and node attributes in synthetic data, outperforming algorithms focused solely on the network or attributes when neither are very informative. Multiple rounds of learning also improve the performance and always outperforms a long single round of training (i.e., classic GNN graph clustering). When considering real datasets, empirical results indicate that the proposed methodology is competitive to state-of-the-art methods when cluster sizes are balanced.

Motivation: 现有的3D分子生成扩散模型缺乏一种原则性的机制来评估生成样本的质量，导致用户难以识别低质量的分子。因此，作者旨在提出一种通用的后验方法来估计分子生成过程中的不确定性。

Method: 基于预训练分子扩散模型的去噪网络，采用拉普拉斯近似（Laplace approximation）方法，通过测量去噪过程中噪声预测的变异性（variability）来估算单样本的不确定性得分。

Result: 实验表明，所提出的不确定性得分与既有的分子质量评价指标呈负相关；通过利用该指标进行测试时筛选（test-time filtering），可以有效剔除低质量样本，从而提升模型的整体生成性能。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种针对预训练分子扩散模型的后验不确定性估计方法，证明了基于拉普拉斯近似的去噪轨迹差异化能够有效量化生成分子的质量，并证实了该指标在筛选高质量分子以提升模型整体性能方面的实用价值。

Abstract: Diffusion models have seen wide adoption for 3D molecular generation, yet they offer no principled signal of when a generated molecule is likely to be of low quality. We propose a post-hoc method for estimating per-sample uncertainty in pretrained molecular diffusion models. Building on a Laplace approximation of the denoising network, we measure the variability of the noise prediction across the generation trajectory. Empirically, we show that the resulting uncertainty score is informative of sample quality, exhibiting a negative correlation with established sample-level quality metrics. We further study how the proposed uncertainty score can be used to filter generated samples, improving model performance via test-time scaling.

### [272] [Reinforcement Learning for Neural Model Editing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13461)
*Shaivi Malik*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统针对特定目标的神经模型编辑需要设计专门的算法，这一过程耗时且费力。为了解决这一痛点，作者旨在构建一个通用的框架，通过强化学习让智能体自主学习模型编辑策略。

Method: 提出了一种将神经模型编辑建模为强化学习问题的框架，引入了两个操作环境：MaskWorld（通过乘法缩放权重）和ShiftWorld（通过加法更新权重）。通过结合效用保留目标和特定任务编辑目标的奖励函数，训练智能体自动学习模型修改策略，从而在实现目标的同时保持整体模型性能。

Result: 在图像分类的机器遗忘任务中，智能体能够将遗忘集准确率降至近0%，同时保留超过90%的保留集准确率；在文本分类的偏差缓解任务中，偏差相关性能提升了超过5%，且基本维持了原有的分类效用。

Conclusion: 本文成功证明了神经模型编辑可以被建模为强化学习问题。这种基于奖励反馈的学习策略避免了为特定编辑任务手动设计算法的繁琐过程，为模型编辑提供了一种通用且高效的新范式。

Abstract: Editing pretrained neural networks requires specialized algorithms tailored to specific objectives. Designing such algorithms is often time-consuming and demands significant effort. We present an exploratory framework that formulates neural model editing as a reinforcement learning problem, where agents modify models using reward feedback. We introduce two environments: MaskWorld, where agents scale weights multiplicatively, and ShiftWorld, where agents apply additive weight updates. The reward function combines a utility-preservation objective with a task-specific editing objective, enabling agents to learn targeted modifications while maintaining overall model performance. We evaluate the framework on bias mitigation in text classification and machine unlearning in image classification, both of which traditionally rely on specialized algorithms. Our results show that the learned policies reduce forget set accuracy to nearly 0% while preserving over 90% retain set accuracy on the unlearning task. In the bias mitigation setting, the learned policies improve bias-related performance by more than 5% while maintaining general classification utility. Our findings show that neural model editing can be cast as a reinforcement learning problem, allowing editing policies to be learned from reward feedback rather than manually engineered for each task.

### [273] [CRAFTIIF: Cross-Resolution Analytic Four-Type Interpretable Isolation Forest for Multivariate Time Series Anomaly Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13486)
*William Smits*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: CRAFTIIF 是一种创新的无监督多变量时间序列异常检测框架，通过结合多分辨率小波分析与模块化隔离森林，能够有效且可解释地识别四种主要的异常类型，在 mTSBench 基准测试中排名第一，实现了卓越的检测性能与自动归因能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多变量时间序列异常检测方法往往只针对单一或少数几种异常类型（如点异常、分布偏移、时间节律改变或集体相关性破坏），且缺乏必要的解释性，难以在多种实际场景中通用。为了填补这一空白，研究团队旨在开发一种无需针对特定数据集进行调优、且能够同时处理这四种异构异常并提供直接归因解释的无监督通用框架。

Method: CRAFTIIF 框架采用了一种“分而治之”的策略：1. 特征工程：利用四种不同的小波家族（Morlet, DOG, Haar, Coiflet）生成 K=500 个随机分析特征，分别对应四种结构化异常；2. 模型架构：采用五个结构化的隔离森林（Isolation Forest, IF）协同工作，其中四个 IF 分别对应特定异常类型，第五个为元（Meta）IF 处理复杂异常；3. 自适应阈值：集成 Otsu 和 MAD 算法实现无需人工调参的自动阈值校准。该方法通过模块化的 IF 分支，实现了检测过程即是解释过程的特性。

Result: 在 mTSBench 的 19 个数据集评估中，CRAFTIIF 表现出色：F1 分数达到 0.228（全集）和 0.322（可检测子集），在 VUS-PR 指标上以 0.463 的成绩位居所有 25 种对比方法之首，较先前最优方法提升了 40.7%。消融实验证实了其自适应阈值、四分支结构以及元 IF 模块在提升性能方面的关键贡献。此外，该研究识别出 19 个数据集中的 6 个为现有无监督方法无法检测的极限案例。

Conclusion: CRAFTIIF 成功构建了一个能够同时识别四种不同类型异常的全自动化、高可解释性多变量时间序列异常检测框架。研究证明，通过针对性的多分辨率小波特征提取与模块化隔离森林架构，不仅能显著提升检测性能，还能直接从模型结构层面实现异常归因，无需后处理解释。此外，该研究提出的诊断框架揭示了当前基准测试中部分数据集的本质不可检测性，为未来的异常检测研究提供了评估范式。

Abstract: Anomaly detection in multivariate time series is challenged by four structurally distinct anomaly types -- point (isolated spikes), distributional (level shifts), temporal (rhythm changes), and collective (inter-sensor correlation breakdowns) -- each requiring different feature representations. Most unsupervised methods target only one or two types and provide limited interpretability. We present CRAFTIIF (Cross-Resolution Analytic Four-Type Interpretable Isolation Forest), a fully unsupervised framework targeting all four types without dataset-specific tuning. CRAFTIIF generates K=500 random analytic wavelet feature draws across four families (Morlet, DOG, Haar, Coiflet), each targeting a specific anomaly type, feeding five structured Isolation Forests -- one per type plus a meta-IF for compound anomalies. An adaptive Otsu/MAD threshold calibrates detection automatically across anomaly rates from 0.1% to 69.2%. Because each IF is trained exclusively on type-specific features, branch firing provides direct anomaly-type attribution by construction, without post-hoc explanation. Evaluated on all 19 datasets of the mTSBench benchmark (Zhou et al., TMLR 2026), CRAFTIIF achieves mean F1=0.228 (all 19 datasets) and F1=0.322 (13 detectable datasets), ranking first among all 25 evaluated methods on VUS-PR (0.463 vs. previous best 0.329, +40.7%). A diagnostic framework -- oracle F1, detectability limits, and branch separation ratios -- identifies 6 of 19 datasets as fundamentally undetectable by any unsupervised method. Ablation over 11 conditions confirms adaptive thresholding (+38% F1), four-branch structure (+20%), and meta-IF (+23%) are each essential. Code: https://github.com/smitswil/craftiif

</details>


### [274] [A2D2: Fine-Tuning Any-Length Discrete Diffusion for Adaptive Decoding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13565)
*Sophia Tang,Yuchen Zhu,Molei Tao,Pranam Chatterjee*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文提出了A2D2框架，通过联合优化插入（insertion）和去掩码（unmasking）策略进行奖励引导微调。主要技术创新点包括：1) 推导出联合路径测度的Radon-Nikodym导数，在无需目标样本的情况下实现向奖励倾斜分布的收敛；2) 将去掩码与插入质量作为最小化解码误差的手段；3) 引入自适应联合解码（AJD）损失函数，实现最优路径测度优化。
